<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kopyto</i>, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱoph₂ós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:копыто.html>копы́то</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kopýto</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:копыто.html>копы́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:копыто.html>копы́та</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:копыто.html>копы́т</a></b>)
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:копящий.html>копя́щий</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:копящий.html>ко́пящий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kopjáščij</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kópjaščij</span>)

***кора.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кора.html>кора</a> (5994)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:кора.html>кора</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kora</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bark</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kora</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bark</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)ker-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кора.html>кора́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">korá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кора.html>коры́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1d |   <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> мн. ч. предположительны <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> неупотребимы.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:корабельный.html>корабе́льный</a> (12569)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>кора́бль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koráblʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корабельный.html>корабе́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">korabélʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ship; naval
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:корабельный.html>корабе́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:инженер.html>инжене́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>korabélʹnyj</b> inženér</i> ― <span class="e-translation">naval architect</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:корабельный.html>корабе́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мастер.html>ма́стер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>korabélʹnyj</b> máster</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shipwright</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:корабельный.html>корабе́льная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:авиация.html>авиа́ция</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>korabélʹnaja</b> aviácija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shipborne aircraft</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:корабельный.html>корабе́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>korabélʹnyj</b> les</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ship timber</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***корабль.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>кора́бль</a> (1013)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>кора́бль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">korablĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*korabľь</i>, old borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">καράβιον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">karábion</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κάραβος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kárabos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">caravel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>кора́бль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">koráblʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>корабля́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>корабли́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>корабле́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ship, liner
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:списывать.html>спи́сывать</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:списать.html>списа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>корабля́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">spísyvatʹ/spisátʹ s <b>korabljá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to transfer/post from <b>a ship</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">formally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> warship</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nave</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> match box for marijuana, by consonance with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коробка.html>коробок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">korobok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In modern technical and formal usage, <a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>кора́бль</a> refers to warships. Informally, can refer to various large ships. Historically, referred to square-rigged sailing ships, similarly to the historical sense of the English word "ship".</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коралл.html>кора́лл</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">koráll</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коралл.html>кора́лла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коралл.html>кора́ллы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коралловый.html>кора́ллов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коралловый.html>кора́лловый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>coral
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">Карл <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> кла́ры <a href = vnd.unilang:украсть.html>укра́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:коралл.html>кора́ллы</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> кла́ра <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> ка́рла <a href = vnd.unilang:украсть.html>укра́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кларнет.html>кларне́т</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Karl u Kláry ukrál <b>korálly</b>, a Klára u Kárla ukrála klarnét.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><i>Carl stole corals from Clara, then Clara stole a clarinet from Carl.</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a> Russian tongue-twister)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коралловый.html>кора́лловый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">korállovyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> coral
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:коралловый.html>кора́лловый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:риф.html>риф</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>korállovyj</b> rif</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>coral</b> reef</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:коралловый.html>кора́лловая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сережка.html>серёжка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>korállovaja</b> serjóžka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>coral</b> earring</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:корежить.html>корёжить</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — скорёжить, <a href = vnd.unilang:искорежить.html>искорёжить</a>, покорёжить.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-корёж-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kórenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корённый.html>коренно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">korennój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>indigenous, native, aboriginal</li>
<li>fundamental, radical, basic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:корённый.html>коренно́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:преобразование.html>преобразова́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>korennóje</b> preobrazovánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">radical change, fundamental change</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:корённый.html>коренно́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перелом.html>перело́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>korennój</b> perelóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">radical turn</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:корённый.html>коренны́м</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:образ.html>о́бразом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>korenným</b> óbrazom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">radically, fundamentally</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:корённый.html>коренны́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́сы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>korennýje</b> interésy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">vital interests</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кореянка.html>корея́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">korejánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кореянка.html>корея́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кореянка.html>корея́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кореянка.html>корея́нок</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кореец.html>коре́ец</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:корить.html>кори́ть</a> (17693)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*korìti</i>. Synchronically, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:кора.html>ко́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kor</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">swearword, offence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корить.html>кори́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">korítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to reproach <i>(with)</i>, to upbraid <i>(with, for)</i></li>
<li>to cast in someone's teeth</li></ol>

***коричневый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:коричневый.html>кори́чневый</a> (2307)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кори́ца</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koríca</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cinnamon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коричневый.html>кори́чневый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">koríčnevyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>brown
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:коричневый.html>кори́чневый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>са́хар</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>koríčnevyj</b> sáxar</i> ― <span class="e-translation">brown sugar</span></div></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ultra-nationalistic, fascist, far right-wing, jingoist</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>For eye color, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карий.html>ка́рий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kárij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> should be used instead. For brown bears and some other animal species names, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурый.html>бу́рый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">búryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> should be used instead.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кори́ца</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">koríca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коричневатый.html>коричнева́тый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">koričnevatyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">коричневеть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">koričnevetʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:корм.html>корм</a> (6238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">кърмъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kŭrmŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kъrmъ</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корм.html>корм</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">korm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корм.html>ко́рма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корм.html>корма́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корм.html>кормо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>feed, fodder, food for animals</li>
<li>the act of feeding</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кормежка.html>кормёжка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kormjóžka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span>

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кормежка.html>кормёжка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kormjóžka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кора.html>ко́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>мёж<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
